Multiple Level IV violations may collectively be considered a breach of conduct.\n\nLevel IV: Incidental Issues\n\nMinor infractions that are inadvertent and isolated, technical in nature and result in a negligible, if any, competitive advantage. Level IV infractions generally will not affect eligibility for intercollegiate athletics.
